2a1(1): thugs gsang ba'i ye shes/ don gyi stong pa khra ba
2a2(1): rigs/ kun 'dus rig pa'i mdol/ rnal 'byor bsgrub pa'i rlud zhes bya ba theg pa

2a4(1): skad bdag gi tho ba'i dus gcig na/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis bcom ldan 'das
2b1(1): dpal kun tu bzang po rdo rjes he ru ka gsang ba mchog bdag po byin gyi brlabs kyi dbang phyug/ myi zang
2b2(1): mdzod kyi bkod pa/ che ba'i don la dam pa'i spyod pa chen pos bskyed pa de/ rlung du byung ba'i don 'ang
2b3(1): zhing bshad pa'i gnas gas rabasang ba/ kun gzhi chos kyi dbyings kyi pho brangs/ thig le
2b4(1): blang lnga ba'i klong / ye 'byam pa rlung du gragaso pa'i gzhal yas rgya bcur yongs su ma chad pa/ rno
2b5(1): nyid kyi nam mkha' las cho 'phrul gyi sprin kun tu 'thibs pa/ byang chub kyi char mngon par 'bab pa
5a1(1): 'khor ba la 'di lta ste/ gsang ba chen mo byams pa'i snying po zhes bya ba'i sangs rgyas dang / gsang ba chen po'i snying po zhes bya ba'i sangs rgyas dang / gsang ba ni
5a2(1): ba chen po dga' ba'i snying po zhes bya ba'i sangs rgyas dang / gsang ba chen po snyoms par gyi snying po zhes bya ba'i sangs rgyas dang / bsang ba chen po bde ba'i dbang phyug ma zhes bya ba'i rnal
5a3(1): 'byor ma chen mo dang / gsang ba chen mo 'joms byed dbang phyug ma zhes bya ba'i rnal 'byor ma chen mo dang / gsang ba chen mo dga'i ba'i dbang phyug ma chen mo dang / gsang ba chen mo khyab
5a4(1): pa'i dbang phyug ma zhes bya ba'i dbang phyug chen mo la stsogs ste/ shin tu tshad myed pa'i 'khor dang / gzhan yang rol pa chen po'i 'khor 'di lta ste/ rol pa chen po sangs rgya ya k+Sha he ru
5a5(1): ka zhes bya ba dang / rol pa chen po sangs rgyas rak+Sha he ru ka zhes bya ba dang / rol bachen po sangs rgyas byig sha he ru zhes bya ba dang / rol pa chen po rnal 'byor ma yak+ShA shwa ri ka nas bya ba
5a6(1): dang / rol pa chen po'i rmil 'byor ma rak+Sha shA rI ga zhes bya ba dang / rol pa chen po'i rnal 'byor ma b+h+r-ig kA rI ga nyis bya ba dang / rol pa chen mo'i rnal 'byor ma hrI shi shU ka zhes bya ba
5a7(1): la stsogs te/ shin du rol pa chen po 'khor dang / gzhan yang 'jig byed chen po'i sangs rgyas te ga bai ru ka zhes bya ba dang / 'jigs byed chen po'i sing sa rgyas ke sha he ru ka zhes byab
5a8(1): ngang 'dres byed chen po'i sangs rgyas 'jigs byed can po'i rnal 'byor mo pa shA ri gzhes bya ba dang / 'jigs byeng chen mo'o rnal 'byor mako bA gzhes bya ba dang bu ba dang / 'dzi so// 
5b1(1): byed chen mo'i 'byor ma pi kA ri zhes bya ba dang / 'joms byed chen popo rmi la ma b+hi shA ri ka zhes bya 'as mi na thigs byeng chen po'i 'khor dang / gzhan yang 'joms byed chen po'i 'khor
5b2(1): 'di lta ste 'joms byed chen po'i sangs rgyas trag/ he ru ka ces bya ba dang / 'jigs byed chen po 'khor sangs rgyas rba~M babe ru ga zhes bya ba dang / 'joms byed chen pa'i sangs rgyas
5b3(1): ru zhes bya ba dang / 'joms byed chen po'i sangs rgyas b+ha k+ShA he ru ka nas bya ba dang / 'joms byed chen po'i rnal 'byor ma trag sha shwa ri ka zhes bya ba dang / 'joms byed chen po'i rnal 'byor ma
5b4(1): hri sha shwa ri ka zhes bya ba dang / 'joms byed chen po'i rnal 'byor ma ka sha shwa ri ka zhes bya ba dang / 'joms byed chen po'i rnal 'byor ma b+ha kA ri ka la spogs te/ shin tu
5b5(1): 'joms byed chen mo'i 'khor dang / gzhan yang za byed chen po'i 'khor 'di lta ste/ za byed chen po'i sangs rgyas ru ti he ru ka zhes bya ba dang / za byed chen mo'i sangs rgyas rag
5b6(1): ti he ru ka zhes bya ba dang / za byed chen po'i sangs rgyas kha hi he ru ka zhes bya ba dang / za byed chen po'i sangs rgyas sa he ru ka zhes bya ba dang / za byed chen po'i rnam 'byor ma ru tik+Sha ri ka zhes
5b7(1): bya ba dang / za byed chen po'i rnal 'byor ma rag ti shwa rI ka zhes bya ba dang / za byed chen po'i rnal 'byor ma kha hi shwa ri zhes bya ba dang / za byed chen mo'i rnal 'byor ma sa hA shwa ri ka zhes bya ba
5b8(1): la spogs te/ rnal 'byor gyi 'khor rab tu mang zhing bsam gyis myi khyab pa'i hi ka mtha' yas pa sha stag rnams dang / gzhan yang gsang ba'i bu mo'i 'khor 'di lta ste/ gsang
8a1(1): pa bzhengs su gsol/ de nas bcom ldan 'das gsang ba mchog gi bdag po ngos cho 'phrul 'byung ba'i glu des gsol ba btab par mkhyen nas
8a2(1): rdo rje rol pa de kho na nyid ces bya ba'i ting 'dzin la snyoms par bzhugs nas cang myi gsung bar bzhugs so// de nas yum kun tu bzang mi dang gnyis su myed par khyab par cang myi
8a3(1): gsung bar bzhugs pa de la/ dam tshig chen po rdo rje sems dpa' la stsogs pa 'khor shin tu mang po rnams ngo mtshar du gyur te// de dag thams cad mgrin cig tu rdo rje rol pa de kha'i
8a4(1): glu 'dis bskul te gsol ba btab po// e ma'o yid bzhin sku mchog na mkha' lta bu las// khyab pa'i byin brlabs rdo rje gar mdzad cing / gzi brjid sprin phung rol pas bgyings
8a5(1): pa'i sku// thog myed rdo rje rol pa'i cho 'phrul ston// e ma ho yid bzhin gsung mchog sma rnyan lta bu las// sman pa'i byin brlabs rdo rje brjod mdzad cing // yan lag rgya mtsho myi zang bkang bani
8a6(1): gsung // seng ge'i sgra'i gsung sngags rgya mtsho ston// e ma ho ye shes snying po nyi ma lta bu las// ye shes byin brlabs rdo rje bde mdzad cing // thig le spros bral rnam par myi rtog thugs
8a7(1): rnam grol de nyid nges pa'i cho 'phrul ston// myi shes blun rmongs 'dam 'byings 'gro ba rnams// sdug bsngal rgya mtshos bcings pa thabs kyis grol// ma rig mun pa ldongs pa don gyi skye
8a8(1): 'khor ba'i rgya mtshor rol pa'i gru yi snol// de bzhin gshegs pa kun gyi thugs chen po// ye shes rgyal ba don snying po mchog dang ldan// rnal 'byor chen po rdo rje kun 'dus rgyud/ 'dus pa sna tshogs
8b1(1): largya cher bshad du gsol// e mtsho zhes nges par bdud te gsol ba btab bo// de nas bcom ldan 'das bsang ba mchog gi bdag po ngas rdo rje rol pa'i de kho na nyid kyi glu nges gsol pa btab mkhyen
8b2(1): nas 'khor thams cad lta gzigs te 'dzum pa mdzad ngas/ thugs rnam par dag pa'i blong nas rig pa'i nyim brjod pa kyis myi lang ba'i 'od gzer dang bcas pa dang / 'byam klas pa'i khyab pa
8b3(1): khung par shar bar mdzad do// 'od gzer de dag re re las rdo rje he ru ka rab tu mang po'i tshogs shar bar mdzad do// de dag re re las kyang sangs rgyas 'bum phrag 'khor so so'i zhabs 'bring rang bcas pa
8b4(1): lhun gyi grub par mdzad do// de dag las rig pa'i nyi ma'i char mngon par phags pas/ mun pa'i klong thams cad gsal mdzad de/ rig pa'i chos kyi 'brug sgra dang / rig pa'i chos kyi char dang / 
8b5(1): rig pa'i chos kyi glu sna tshogs pa dang / gar sna tshogs dang / rig pa'i chos kyi mchod pa sna tshogs phul ste/ dbyam klas pa'i na mkha' la/ sgra sna tshogs phan tshun dang / yin man dang / 
8b6(1): spel ba ni la stsogs pa thams cad du khyab par ling long phung bar phyung ngo // mchod pa'i char yang mngon par phab bo// rmang du 'brang ba'i sku bsam gyis myi khyab pa yang ling long 'byung / nang
8b7(1): du byung ba'i thugs kyang lha de'o// rmad du byung ba'i gsung bsam gyi myi khyab pa a la a la la to/ sgra sgrogs sangs rgyas 'bum phrag kyang gsung dbyangs bsam gyi myi khyab pa'i sgra cig
8b8(1): du s+yas/ e mdo rmang du byung ba rol pa chos kyi ngor byung ngo // zhes sgrogs sa// 'khor 'bum phrag dag dang / gdul bya sna tshogs spro ba'i ngo mtshar bskyed/ rig pa'i rtsal sbyangs/ don
10a1(1): rdo rje rgyal po'i tshogs bdag dgongs su gsol/ chos kyi rgyal po myi g.yo rgyal tshul mdzad// rgyal mcho ga rgyal pos chos kyi rgyal po'i sku// 'dus
10a2(1): pa'i tshogs la/ rgya cher bshad du gsol/ a la la ho/ zhes gsol ba btab pa las bcom ldan 'das gsang ba mchog gi bdag po ngos/ rdo rje las bka' ba byin gyis brlabs pa'i
10a3(1): phyir/ rdo rje rnam par spro bzhis bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// badz+ra karbArma kra sa ta ma ram zhes gsungs te/ rdo rje rgya bram 'khor long man gcig
10a4(1): sems pa rdo rje'i lag babs par gyur nas/ las kyi rdo rje'i dbang thob par gyurd te/ rnam par rol pa chen po shin tu bkra bkyil ba'i spobs pacad du byin gyis brlabs nas/ kun tu myi
10a5(1): bzod rab tu bag dang ldan pa chen por gyur to// de nas sems dpa' rdo rje des// las kyi mtshan de lag tu blangs te/ stabs sna tshogs dang / gar dang / klu sna tshogs dang / rdo rje
10a6(1): tshig tu len cing / rdo rje rgya gram las kyi 'khor de lan rnam pa lnga lnga ste/ bcu gnyis gnyis dang lnga lngar bsgyur bas zhing khams mtha' dag rnam par g.yos te/ g.yos/ kun du rab tu g.yos/ 
10a7(1): 'gul/ rab tu 'gul/ kun tu rab tu 'gul/ ldeg rab tu ldeg shun tun rab ldeg/ 'khrugs rab tu 'khrugs/ kun tu rab tu 'khrugs/ bur rab tu 'ur/ kun tu rab tu 'ur/ 
10a8(1): chem rab tu mtsham/ kun tu rab tu chem khar 'gyur te/ zhing thams cad ni gsang ba'i dkyil 'khor she dag tu byur/ bcud dang yul thams cad ni phyag rgya chen por gyur te/ rnam par rngam pa ni
10b1(1): tshul gyis ston pa'i mdun logs su seng ge'i khri rdo rjes mtshan pa'i gdan la 'gying bag gi tshul gyis rnam par gnas so// de nas 'dus pa'i 'khor tshogs phal mo che rnams kyis/ 
10b2(1): bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol te/ e mdo/ bcom ldan 'das sems dpa' rdo rje 'di ni 'di ni 'di ltar mthu che ba 'di ltar byin brlabs che ba/ 'di ltar rgya che ba
10b3(1): 'di ltar gsal zhing zab pa ni/ bcom ldan 'das kyi thugs sras lags so// ces gsol pa dang / bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ 'dus pa chen po'i tshogs
10b4(1): sems dpa' rdo rje 'di ni byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi phyi mo/ snying rje thams cad kyi bdag po/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rje ba tsan/ byang chub sems dpa' rigs 'dzin
10b5(1): thams cad kyi yab/ rnal 'byor thams cad kyi myes chen po/ mya ngan las 'das pa thams cad kyi ded dpon/ bdud thams cad kyi yang bdud chen po/ chos thams cad kyi mdzod
10b6(1): ye shes thams cad kyi 'byung gnas/ chen por gyu rad pa yin no// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ thog ma tha ma myed par mnyam pa'i dus/ pa tha las kyang pha mtha'/ dpag tu myed cing
10b7(1): bsam du myed pa/ 'byam bklas pa'i dus nas/ bya ba byas shing byed pa bya ba/ mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas pa yin te/ chos thams cad kyi rang bzhin du sbyor zhing / gnas pas
10b8(1): nas rgyal ba thams cad kyi thugs las skyes shing / thams cad kyi thugs yab tu gyu rad pa yin te/ de 'dra'o// zhes bka' stsal pa las/ 'dus pa'i 'khor thams cad kyi rang
11a1(1): ngo mtshar du gyu ra te/ bcom ldan 'das 'dis ni 'di ltar ngo mtshar lags/ zhes gsol te/ sems dpa' rdo rje dam pa lags su btud te/

11a4(1): mchog dam pa dag/ tshig gis mtshon te gsal bar mdzad// a la la 'o// zhes gsol ba btab po/ de nas dam pa rdo rjes rdo rje skor te sbyar nas/ brjid bag du tshig tu mtshon
11a5(1): smras pa oM a hUM/ a la laso/ rgyal ba'i sras po bcang myi gsungasamyi gsung bas ni rgya cher bshad// bshad du myed pa'i chos 'di ni// rgyal ba rnams kyis ma bshad de// de ltar
11a6(1): ston pa'i rgyal mchog kyang // rnam par brjod par myi bamed de/ rgya cher bshad par dgongs po// skye ba med pa'i chos rnams ni// ma skyes pa'ang snying por bshad// snying pa'i don du gang
11a7(1): gyur pa// tshig tu smras pa logs ma yin// spros pa zhid na gol ba myed zhes// rgyal ba rnams kyis yang dag bshad// de bas rdo rje rgyal po nyid// bka' ma stsal bar
11a8(1): dgongs pa'o// dgongs pa'i don rnams gang 'byin pa// ci ltar mye long gzugs rnyan ltar// dgongs don rigs la bsal gyu rang ba// ma skyes snying po'i don gyi gnas// 
11b1(1): tshig tu smos pa ma yin yang // mtshan mtshig gi rnal 'byor pa// tshig la zhib la don la cing // tshig byer blo 'brangs rtsal gzhan rnams// bkri phyir bsam pa rangs rgyu
11b2(1): // myi dmyigs pa la dmyigs pa dang // cho 'phrul tshig gis mtshon pa ni// bde bshegs rgyal ba kun thugs// gsang ba de nyid snying po'i don// mnyam nyid byang chub zog
11b3(1): chen po// gsal bar bkod pa des brjod kyis/ rgya chen 'dus pa'i tshogs rnams nyon// nga ni dus gsum bzugs pa yi// rgyal ba kun gyi snying po ste// stong bar sbas pa'i
11b4(1): don 'di la// dpes mtshon tshig gi lde myig gyis// mnyam pa nying rig pa'i stong bye byas// sbas pa'i don 'byin gsal byed pa// sa lu'i phub khrod snang mye bzhin
11b5(1): gsal dag snang skye sa ler 'dug/ zab mor spyod pa la mos pa// gang zhig don la dris pa yi// gsang bsngags spyod pa'i rang bzhin ni// mthun pa'i dmyigs bcu
11b6(1): dper bzhag ste// rnal 'byor can gyis shes par bya// sgyu ma smyig rgyu rmi lam dang // gzugs brnyan dri za'i grong khyer dang // brag cha chu zla myig g.yor dang // chu bur
11b7(1): 'khrul dang 'gal myer snang // sgrub dang gsang sngags spyod pa dang // grub pa dang ni gnas dag dang // zlas pa'i sgra dang phyag rgyar rtog/ ting 'dzin lta ba cho 'phrul rtag
11b8(1): ci ltar sgyu ma'i mtshan nyid ni// skyes bu dag gi stsol ba dang // sman dang sngags kyi sbyor ba las// dbang po'i yid 'phrog cir yang snang // de la 'gro 'ong ga la yod// de ltar
12a1(1): sgrub pa'i mnam kyang / sa rgyangs kyi sbyor ba las/ chub par snang yang rang ba chud/  byung chu // nang ba nga
12a2(1): kyis zla ba las/ drod dang ni ma'i sbyor ba las// byis pa gdungs pa'i rang bzhin gyis/ chu'i 'du shes ci basbrid kyang // skom pa'i sbur ni ga la 'gyur/ gsang sngags mying gi khyang bar

12a4(1): yud tsam cig dang / lo la stsogs pa de bzhin du/ bde dang sngags bsngal de bzhin myong // sangs nas ci yang myi dmyigs ltar/ de bzhin sngags kyi sbyong ba dang // stong pa nyid kyi rang bzhin las
12a5(1): spyod pa rnam par cir yang / brtags na dmyigs pa kun dang bral// gzugs rnyan snang ba'i bzhin ni// dper na rdong dang myi long la// bstan nA rang bzhin gzugs 'byung yang // do bar
12a6(1): gyur pa ga la yong// / de bzhin sngags kyi dngos grub kyang / grub nas ting 'dzin yong byad las// rten nas dngos grub tshul yang // gsol thob dmyigs pa ga la yod// dri nga gnas pa'i
12a7(1): ngang na no// mkhar yang spong ba'i ngos dgal// dri'i gzungs ni par byung // grong khyer de yang de las byung // bung nas de yang mu rtag la dang gsang sngabs thub pa'i gnas ngag kya
12a8(1): chos sam yid kyi mkha' nges la// rnal 'byor gsang bdag la/ gar bskyed par// de nyid gnas pa'i gzhal yas khang // 'byung yang de la gnas myi 'gyur// brag ma grags pa'i mtshan
12b1(1): mam dper na sa las rkye pas/ ci ni sna ltar thab cha ltar// rlung yang sbyar thos dkyikris pazlob de bzhin drags kyig rnas pa'i sa/ ba na mud las yo brnags pa'o/ na
12b2(1): ma la rten stong pa'i sna// brjod pa tsam du sman par zad// ji ltar chu'i zla ba ni// sgrib myed mkha' la zla shar ba// gzugs brtan dang ba'i chu nang snang // snang yang gzung ba'i rtog pa myed/ 
12b3(1): de bzhin gzugs snang phyag rgya yang // sems kyi mkha' las skur gsal ba// phyag rgya'i rigs 'dzin ngo la snang // de ltar snang 'dzin rtog pa bral// ji ltar char gyi rgyun bzhin du// chu la chu bur rnam pa
12b4(1): byung // de yang gcig gi rnam pa las// mang po'i rnam grangs dum la byung // srung cing phyir yang du mchad// de bzhin rnal 'byor sgrub pa yi// ting nge 'dzin rnams mang por 'dod// 'khrul
12b5(1): bsnang ba'i rang bzhin ni// spos bral dngos po stong pa// srog dang shed can byed pa bo// sems can pa la stsogs par snang // dmug nang ngo la rdzas ltar sdang // 'khrul pa kho nar snang bar zad
12b6(1): de bzhin sngags kyi lta ba yang // cho 'phrul mang po cir sprul yang // snang ba myed pa'i rang bzhin las// 'khrul pa sna chags snang bar zad// dmyig nang ngo la rdzas ltar snang / rnal 'byor
12b7(1): can gyis de ltar lta ci ltar 'gal mye'i rang bzhin ni// gang dag lag na 'gal mye thogs// skor na 'khor lo'i rgyun ltar snang // de la 'khor rang bzhin myed// de bzhin sngags kyi cho 'phrul
12b8(1): yang myi mnyam pa'i rang bzhin las// ci ltar dmyigs pa rje rang bzhin 'brang so// cho 'phrul sna tshogs rgyun gyi ched/ de bzhin mtshan ma'i chos thams cad mtshan nyid dang du gcig pas ma/ 
13a1(1): rtog pa'i bag chags ci 'byung yang // chos kun dbyings su gcig 'byung ba'i phyir// rtog 'jug spros pa'i mtshan ma ma kun// ma byung ma skyes dbyings lnga/ 
13a2(1): g.yos pa myed cing cho 'phrul 'byung // yon tan sna tshogs cher 'byung gter gyi dbyig 'di gang mthong ba// sangs rgyas kun gyi yon tan yang // skad cig gcig la de la 'dus/ de bas yid rin chen
13a3(1): 'didi ldog pa myed pa'i ding du blang // don dam yang dag gter gyi mchog/ rnal 'byor kun gyi nor mchog ste// gang brtags de thob gcig pu nyid// 'brel myed gzhan gyis thob par dka'
13a4(1): bdag myed gnyis bral bde chen klong // sangs rgyas kun gyi bde ba che// ye nas lhun 'grub 'dus ma byas// thig le chos nyid ye 'bum pa// kun khyab bdal bas snying por 'dus// 
13a5(1): myi dmyigs spos bral byang chub sems zab mo snang ba'i nges pa 'di// mkha' la 'dug 'dra gting dpag dkar// rnal 'byor myi ldan blo chung zhing // gang zhig dpal zhan te rtogs pa/ 
13a6(1): g.yod mo'i tshul du bdag rtags pa// rtags kyang rtag par myi 'gyur ro// dper na nyi ma'i snying po la// myig gi dbang pos rab rdugs na// de brtags don myed kyi rtogs kyi// 'od
13a7(1): kyi gzer gyis dmyigs rdzi 'gyur/ de 'dra byis pa'i rang bzhin gyis// zab mo'i don la cir brtags kyang // yang dag don de mi mthong gi/ blo nan byis pa gachang rgyal// brtag tu myed pa 'i
13a8(1): chos rnams ni// rtogs pa can gyis ma rtog te// gang zhig don myi rtogs phyir// yangs sar lhung btsam yod// gdonas ma thos shin tu dge// bsam pa dang bral bas de bzhin bzhag/ myi rtog
13b1(1): skyo nobs bzhug pa ma chos 'di dang // bris pa rnams la ngas ma snus// banan kyang go bar myi 'gyur te// bsnyur du myed cing go bar dka' tshig gis brjod pa kun dang bral// 'di nas
13b2(1): bstan dug yod// myed pa bstan pa'i zugs myi bri// myi dbyigs chos la blo sbyangs shing // yid kyi myi 'dzegs la bus ma// mamakha' bdag la rab brnabs na// snang med par
13b3(1): rang bzhin 'di// na mkha' lta bur de nyid 'gyur// chos nyid namakha' lta bu ste// namakha' la yang mtshan nyid myed// nam mkha' gang mying brjod byed pa// brjod pa de nyid dngos pos
13b4(1): dngos po de'i mying brjod kyang // ma mkha' de la 'gag myi 'gyur// de bzhin myi rtog brjod byed pa// brjod pa de nyid rnam rtog ste// myi rtog de'i mying brjod kyang // myi rtog de la 'gag
13b5(1): myi 'gyur/ de 'drar sems kyang de ltar blta// sems nyid gzhan du ma grub ste// de bzhin chos kyang grub ma yin// sems dang chos nyid gnyis myed de// sems nying bang yin chos nyid de/ 
13b6(1): chos nyid kyang de bzhin no// chos sems gnyis myed ldan gyur pa// bla myed byang chen por bshad// sems ni ma mkha' lta bu ste// rnam par bral gang myi rtog/ de bzhin sa gzhi chen po ltar/ 
13b7(1): bla myed byang chungab myu gu bskyed// mye'i rang bzhin ltar snang bas// rmongs pa'i bud shing bsregs par byed// rlung gi rang bzhin yin pa na// myi shes pa yi rdul kun sel// chu'i rang bzhin yin
13b8(1): ban/ nyon mongs bdung ba kun sel byed// sran gyiring bzhin 'ani bram// 'khor ba'i gcod srid par 'byin// de ltar bu'i rang bzhin pas// 'chi ba rnams kyi gsos su 'bab// de bzhin nongs
14a1(1): rang bzhin pas/ sdug bsngal rgya mtsho rnams par gcod// nyi ma lta bur snang ba'i mun khang snang stong sel bar byed/ ri rab lta bu'i rang bzhin
14a2(1): las// brtan po myi 'gyur g.yo ba myed// rgya mtsho lta bu'i rang bzhin pas// myi g.yo ba la byin rlabs che// sems ni 'di ltar cho 'phrul las// de phyir 'khor ba mya ngan
14a3(1): 'das// gnyis su snang ba ma yin te// sems kyi rang bzhin bzang ngan las// gnyis kyi 'du shes phye ba stan// sems las yang dag ye shes 'byung // de bzhin bde
14a4(1): dang sdug bsngal 'byung // chos dang sangs rgyas ye shes 'byung // dge 'dun yang ni de bzhin no// 'di las pha rol phyin rdzogs dang // byang chub dang ni pad+mo 'byung
14a5(1): 'di las rdo rje sems dpa' dang // dri myed rin dpal sbyin 'byung // de bzhin rdo rje dpag myed dang // sna tshogs rgyal ba 'di las 'byung // 'di las sngags dang phyag rgya stsogs
14a6(1): rig pa'i myed po thams cad 'byung // 'di las 'dod chags zhe sdang dang // sdug bsngal nga rgyal phra dog 'byung // gti mug dag kyang de bzhin te// 'di las khams gsum thams
14a7(1): cad du/ skyes pa rung myed ma ning 'byung // 'di la 'od dang 'od zer 'byung // nyon mongs gdung 'dod chags pa 'byung // ri dang skye bo de bzhin 'byung // namakha' dang ni rlung dag dang / 
14a8(1): bsreg pa'i mu ni rab tu 'byung // 'di las dang chung mi// rdo dang sa bon myu gu 'byung // de bzhin klog dang skar mda' dang // nyi ma'i sbyin rnams 'byung // de bzhin spyod dang mi srong dum
14b1(1): thams cad thams cad 'byung bar 'gyur// dper na namakha'i rang bzhin las// srin dang nabu khu blangs dang / zla ba ba'i'in skar tshogs dog snang yang nam mkha' bzhin du gnas/ 
14b2(1): de bzhin sems kyi mkha' las// mtshan ma'i chos 'phrul ci byung yang // chos nyid nam mkha' bzhin gnas par// rnal 'byor can gyis blta bar bya// de lta bu'i sems nyid ni// rtogs
14b3(1): dang ma rtogs rang bzhin las// lta ba'i khyad par sa sor spong // rtog pa can gyi gang la// rtog pa 'phrul pa'i ngo bor sdang // kun du nyer 'jog lam 'tshal la// kun tu rdul
14b4(1): gyi phung por snang // tshogs spyod snying rje nyer 'jog la// thams cad sgyu ma'i rang bzhin ltar// de ltar nyid mnyam par shes gnas na// mnam kha'i rang bzhin mthong bar gnas// ye shes
14b5(1): rang snang namakha' la// mamakha' zhing du snang bar zad // brjod bral mthong myed dmyings dang bral/ mthong ba myed pa'i don 'di la// sngon gyi rgyal ba rnams kyis bshad// bder
14b6(1): gshegs byang chub snying po la// dgongs pa 'di lnga gang myo mnga'// lta ba de dang ldan bzhin du// dam tshis nam mkha' lta bu la/ bsrung mi bsrung phyogs dang bral/

14b8(1): 'byor pa/ namakha' lta bub dam tshig la// de bsrung du mye na pade// gzhan pa theg pa chung rnams// bsrungs pa'i mtshams dag bsrungs nas ni// skyor yon chos la ba
15a1(1): / ngor byed/ srung dang bral ba'i chos nyid ni// bsrung du myed pas de bzhin bzhag/ de ni bzhin pa'i dam tshig la// ji bzhin pa'i blo gzhag ste/ brjod
15a2(1): pa myed pa'i sems nyid kyis// bsrung ba myed pa'i ngang du brngam// bsrung myed na mkha'i dam tshig 'di// ji ltar grags pa'i rang bzhin la// sdom dang tshul khrims so sor snang /

15a5(1): dam tshig 'di las yod myi mnga'// spyod pa dag pa'i khyad yang // chos nyid bya brtsal kun bral la// bsgrub dang bsgrub pa'i dmyigs myed pa// 'khrul pid+mo skye bo dag/ dmyigs myed byang chub

15a7(1): dpyod// nang na 'dod ha can bsgrub/ tsa sung tsa bsrubs ci brtsal yang // sdug bsnga la da dbyeng nub byud// dbul pas sa rgya chen po'o// sdub bsngal byang chub mi nyid de// nyan

15b1(1): mthong na// bsdub dang brtsal ba ci spang kyang // bris pa'i don myong byin 'khrul// brtsal du med pa'i rang bzhin la// brtsal ba'i sbyor bas tsa zhig bya// 'dzin pa'i rang bzhin la/ 
15b2(1): tshig 'dzin nor ba'i brtsor byar myed/ dgos du myed chos nyid la// dgod pa'i dkyil 'khor mying dang bral// bsam du myed pa'i chos nyid la// rtogs sems bsam pa'i dmyigs dang
15b3(1): bral// brtsal myed ye nas lhur gyis grub// mtha' dbus myed pa'i bdal ba che// phyi nang myed ye gsal khyab// skyon yon myed par lhun gyis rdzogs// bsgrub du myed pa'i

17a1(1): gring ma yis shin tu bsgribs par gyu ra pa ma/ smin rten 'dus pa'i phung po la// kha'i dbugs kyi bus nas/ sprin gsal ni 'od gsal 'dod 'dra// de phyir rnal 'byor dbang phyug gis sems cing
17a2(1): don lam rtogs te/ kun bzhi rtsa ba shes par bya/ sems nyid de la bltas bsal ba// rtsa ba dang ni grang ldan pa// dus dang tshig dang lor gyur mar/ yag galo 'dab 'bras bur bkrun// rtsa ba'i sa bon myed myi 'gyur
